10.7 Removing information from Dictionary

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We created dictionaries, we also learn how to add elements in the
existing dictionary. What if we want to remove some element from the
dictionary permanently ?

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We can easily remove any key by using keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">del.</span> We pass the dictionary name along with
the key. It can delete the key with its value.

</div>

<div id="text00010.html#page_94" class="class_s18A">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s1R6">

del( dictionary\_name \[ key \] )

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Recalling the previous example again, in which we created a dictionary
child having key <span class="class_s4UC">Name, Grade</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Section</span> . Now we want to remove the key <span
class="class_s4UC">Grade</span> from the dictionary child so write as
follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00233.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now when we print child it gives us the following output,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00234.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Note that the key <span class="class_s4UC">Grade</span> with its value
<span class="class_s4UC">Sixth</span> removed from the dictionary.

</div>

</div>

that key is not a part of that dictionary.

</div>

<div class="class_s1R6">

Key in dictionary\_name

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

of outcomes.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

It means to excess every element in the dictionary. Python provides
three methods over dictionary which are

</div>

-   Values
-   Keys
-   <div id="text00010.html#page_96">

    </div>

    Key value pairs

<div class="class_sU4">

We need for loop or while loop for iteration. We will see all the
methods one by one.

10.11 What you can store in Dictionary

</div>

<div class="class_s1WU">

Any data structure can store as value in dictionary. For example

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Dictionary can contain,

</div>

-   <span class="class_s4UK">List</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UK">Tuple</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UK">Any type primitive or user defined</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UK">Another dictionary as its value</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UK">Or combination of these</span>

<div id="text00010.html#a4RA" class="heading_s1X3">

in the list

value is a list, so an extra pair of square brackets is used to access
the list element.

Chapter 11 : Loop

</div>

<div class="class_sJ4">

In general, statements are executed sequentially, first statement
executed then second and so on. Now if we want to perform a task
multiple times we write it multiple times. There may be a situation when
you need to execute a block of code several number of times. For
example, if you want to execute your name for fifty times then you have
to write the statement <span class="class_s4UE">print(name)</span> fifty
times which will definitely take a lot of your time and lines for code.

</div>

<div class="class_s24X-0">

![](Image00292.jpg){.class_s24X-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s24Z">

As your task will be completed by using this method but it is not the
efficient way of doing this.

</div>

<div class="class_s251">

Now, let’s suppose we have a list of different number and we have to
check whether the input value is present in the list or not. In the
following we define a variable <span
class="class_s4UC">Number\_to\_check</span> and assign the integer value
<span class="class_s4UC">7</span> . Also we have a list <span
class="class_s4UC">Number\_list</span> having 5 elements in it,

</div>

<div class="class_s255-0">

![](Image00293.jpg){.class_s255-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s251">

As there are 5 elements in the list so we have to check it for each
element one by one as follows,

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_114" class="class_s25A-1">

![](Image00294.jpg){.class_s25A-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s25C">

As the input 7 is already in the list named <span
class="class_s4UC">Number</span> <span class="class_s4UE">\_</span>
<span class="class_s4UC">list</span> . So this will give us the output
“Yes it is in the list”

</div>

<div class="class_s25A-1">

![](Image00295.jpg){.class_s25A-0}

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#a4RE" class="heading_sJ6">

11.1 For Loop

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

For loop in python is a concise approach. It reduces load of code. The
loop iterate over a given sequence which can be a <span
class="class_s4V5">set, list, tuple</span> or <span
class="class_s4V5">dictionary.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax</span> : We use keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">for(),</span> then create a variable then
sequence(i-e list) and put colon <span class="class_s4UE">(:)</span> to
make a body of loop or intended block.

</div>

<div class="class_s25M">

for a in list:

</div>

<div class="class_sPS">

print(list) \# body of for loop

</div>

<div class="class_sJ4">

Here, the variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> will takes value of
item inside the sequence, in <span id="text00011.html#page_115"></span>
every iteration.

</div>

<div class="class_s251">

We can do previous example using <span class="class_s4UE">for
loop</span> and the function <span class="class_s4UE">range().</span> As
we have to execute the name for fifty times So, we can write as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s251">

![](Image00296.jpg){.class_s25W} It will print the sting <span
class="class_s4UC">John</span> fifty times.

</div>

<div class="class_s260-1">

![](Image00297.jpg){.class_s260-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s251">

As range give values from <span class="class_s4UE">0</span> we can also
generate numbers. If we want to prints till 10<span
class="class_s4UJ">th</span> number, we do as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s265-1">

![](Image00298.jpg){.class_s265-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s251">

We give range of 11 so the loop will iterate eleven times starting
creating values from <span class="class_s4UE">0</span> . In first
iteration the range will create <span class="class_s4UE">0</span> which
will initialize to the variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> . The
<span class="class_s4UE">print statement</span> prints 0.Then in second
iteration, function <span class="class_s4UC">range()</span> create <span
class="class_s4UE">1</span> <span id="text00011.html#page_116"></span>
assign to variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> and prints the
value. Similarly, it will prints the values until the iteration get
completed. Now if we want to print only values from 1 to 5 we can give
the starting and ending point in the range function. We can write as
follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s255-0">

![](Image00299.jpg){.class_s255-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s251">

The loop will execute five times so it prints the values from <span
class="class_s4UC">1</span> to <span class="class_s4UC">5</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s25A-1">

![](Image00300.jpg){.class_s25A-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s25C">

We can also give optional third parameter to the function <span
class="class_s4UE">range()</span> known as step. By default its value is
<span class="class_s4UE">1</span> . In the following, we give the value
to third parameter equals to <span class="class_s4UC">2</span> . It
means that the difference between the two consecutive numbers in the
output will equals to 2. Look!

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_117" class="class_s26J-0">

![](Image00301.jpg){.class_s26J-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s25C">

First it prints the value <span class="class_s4UC">1</span> , then takes
2 steps and prints the value <span class="class_s4UC">3</span> . Again,
it takes two steps and prints <span class="class_s4UC">5</span> and so
on.

</div>

<div class="class_s25C">

Similarly, we can also print the counting in the reverse order starting
the value of range from 10 to 1 and giving step function with negative
value as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s25A-1">

![](Image00302.jpg){.class_s25A-0}

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

We can perform above task related to <span class="class_s4UE">checking
the number</span> in the list by <span class="class_s4UE">for
loop</span> . In the following, we have a variable <span
class="class_s4UC">Number\_to\_check</span> and list <span
class="class_s4UC">Number\_list,</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s1MP-1">

![](Image00303.jpg){.class_s1MP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We apply <span class="class_s4UC">for loop</span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s270-1">

![](Image00304.jpg){.class_s270-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s272">

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_118" class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00305.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

This code pulls up each element in the list <span
class="class_s4UC">Number\_list</span> ,one by one. Note that, we
created a variable <span class="class_s4UC">x</span> in which current
elements in the list will assigned with each iteration. It then checks
this value against the value of the variable <span
class="class_s4UC">Number\_to\_check</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we want to check the number <span class="class_s4UC">7</span> which
we assigned to the variable name <span
class="class_s4UC">Number\_to\_check.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The <span class="class_s4UE">for loop</span> starts with the first
element in the list <span class="class_s4UC">Number\_list</span> . It
asks, Is this first element <span class="class_s4UC">2</span> in the
<span class="class_s4UC">Number\_list</span> <span
id="text00011.html#page_119"></span> , equal to the number we are
checking for? If No, then the loops moves to second number,<span
class="class_s4UC">6.</span> Again it is not equals to <span
class="class_s4UC">7</span> . Then loop moves to third, fourth and so on
until we found the number equals to <span class="class_s4UC">7</span> .
Here fifth number having index\_value <span class="class_s4UC">4</span>
satisfy the equation. So it displays the message "Yes it is in the
list.”

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#a4RF" class="heading_s11B">

11.1.1 Break

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If we want loop to find any specific value in the list having large
number of items but we also want to terminate our loop when it finds the
target value in the list because, after that there is no purpose of
continuing the loop. To terminate the loop python provides the keyword
<span class="class_s4UC">break().</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

For example, we have another list named <span
class="class_s4UC">int</span> having different integer values in it as
follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00306.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Again, we are looking for number <span class="class_s4UC">7</span>
assign to the variable <span class="class_s4UC">Number\_to\_check</span>
. We can write it as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s27K-1">

![](Image00307.jpg){.class_s27K-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here the number <span class="class_s4UC">7</span> have index value of
<span class="class_s4UE">3</span> .So by using <span
class="class_s4UC">break</span> , the loop will be terminated as it
encounters 7.

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_120" class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00308.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here is another example of keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">break().</span> We want to print the number, which
are not divisible by two. So we put a condition that if it’s remainder
equals to zero than break the loop,

</div>

<div class="class_s27W-1">

![](Image00309.jpg){.class_s27W-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we have list having different integer values. When it comes to the
integer value <span class="class_s4UC">60</span> (which is divisible by
2) then, it will break <span class="class_s4UE">for loop</span> and
don’t print any further value whether it satisfy the condition or not.

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#a4RG" class="heading_s11B">

11.1.2 Continue

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If we want to stops only the current iteration but don’t want our loop
to be terminated or exit, we use keyword <span
class="class_s4UC">continue().</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In the following, we have a list <span class="class_s4UE">colors,</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s1MP-1">

![](Image00310.jpg){.class_s1MP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Suppose, we don’t want color <span class="class_s4UC">black</span> to
print. So we use <span class="class_s4UC">continue()</span> to block the
iteration for index value 1.

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_121" class="class_s1KR-0">

![](Image00311.jpg){.class_s1KR-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As the loop don’t exists but print all values except item <span
class="class_s4UC">black</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now we see the same example as we discussed in previous topic <span
class="class_s4UE">break().</span> Now we use keyword <span
class="class_s4UC">continue()</span> instead of <span
class="class_s4UC">break().</span> Iteration in which the condition is
satisfy will be skipped as follows,![](Image00312.jpg){.class_s28D}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here, for loop not printed the value <span class="class_s4UC">60</span>
but after that the loop will continue.

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00313.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

Looking to another example. Now we assign the city names to a list named
<span class="class_s4UC">cities</span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s28P-1">

![](Image00314.jpg){.class_s28P-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We know that we can print each element of the list by using <span
class="class_s4UE">for loop</span> .

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_122" class="class_s27K-1">

![](Image00315.jpg){.class_s27K-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

multiplication table by using the input from user. We stored the input
value in a variable <span class="class_s4UC">table\_number</span> . Now
by running this block of code we get,

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_124" class="class_s1NS-0">

![](Image00321.jpg){.class_s1NS-1}

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00322.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s2A2">

Now, input take value from user and convert it into data type integer.
Then it evaluates the expression inside for loop for ten times as range
is from 1 to 10.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We enter the number <span class="class_s4UC">4</span> .Now <span
class="class_s4UC">4</span> is assigned to the variable <span
class="class_s4UC">table\_number.</span> Then <span
class="class_s4UC">4</span> is multiplied with the values creating by
function <span class="class_s4UC">range()</span> which are from <span
class="class_s4UC">1</span> to <span class="class_s4UC">10</span> .In
this way we get the following multiplication table,

</div>

<div class="class_s2A8">

![](Image00323.jpg){.class_sPY}

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#a4RM" class="heading_s2AA">

11.1.6 Nested for loop:

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The loop within the loop is called <span class="class_s4UE">nested
loop</span> . It means that inner loop is in the body of outer loop.
There is no restriction of defining the inner loops i-e the nesting
level can be defined at n times<span class="class_s4UF">.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

<span class="class_s4UF">The iteration starts from the outer loop which
activates the inner loop. The inner loop executes to completion. After
completion, again second iteration of the outer </span> <span
class="class_s4UG">loop</span> <span class="class_s4UF"> triggers the
inner </span> <span class="class_s4UG">loop</span> <span
class="class_s4UF">. This process repeats until the range of
outer </span> <span class="class_s4UG">loop</span> <span
class="class_s4UF"> finishes. For example, we have the following
block,</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s2AG-0">

![](Image00324.jpg){.class_s2AG-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

When we execute the above block, then the function range will create
number <span class="class_s4UC">0</span> which store in the variable
<span class="class_s4UC">a</span> .Then it prints the <span
class="class_s4UC">print()</span> statement <span
class="class_s4V5">“</span> Inner loop begins” .After that the pointer
will move to the second <span class="class_s4UC">for()</span> loop which
is in the body of first <span class="class_s4UC">for()</span> loop so
whatever is the part of second loop will also execute .

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As there is string value in second <span class="class_s4UC">for()</span>
loop which means it prints the character of the string one by one. It
comes back to the first loop when whole inner body executed. In second
iteration, the function <span class="class_s4UC">range()</span> will
create value of <span class="class_s4UC">1</span> and assign to the
variable <span class="class_s4UC">a.</span> Then prints the <span
class="class_s4UC">print()</span> statement .Again it start the
execution of second loop. It prints the variable <span
class="class_s4UC">a</span> and character of string. The process repeats
again. The output is,

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_126" class="class_s2AP-0">

![](Image00325.jpg){.class_s2AP-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s2AS">

Task:

</div>

programme to display multiple tables (i-e from 2 to 5) at the same time
by using</span> <span class="class_s4UM">nested for() loop</span>

the outer for() will be 2 and input\_value+1 i-e
range(2,input\_value)</span>\

<div id="text00011.html#a4RN" class="heading_sFV">

11.2 While loop

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

This is another type of loop. The while loop works same as <span
class="class_s4V5">for loop</span> . The only difference between them is
that the while loop allow user to terminate the loop by setting the
value of a flag. Flag is just the variable

</div>

<div class="class_s2AZ">

Here we have example,

</div>

<div id="text00011.html#page_127" class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00326.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

First we declare a variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> and set
integer value of <span class="class_s4UC">0</span> to it.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We set the condition of a while loop that if the value of <span
class="class_s4UC">a</span> is less than or equals to zero than print
the following message

</div>

<div class="class_s2B6">

“This is while loop printing”

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As value of <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> satisfied the condition so
it prints the message infinite time 

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we have similar example which we covered in the topic <span
class="class_s4UE">for loop.</span> This will print the number from
<span class="class_s4UE">0</span> to <span class="class_s4UE">5</span>
.We can write the while loop as follows:

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00327.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Again, we declare a variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> and
assign integer value <span class="class_s4UC">0</span> to it.

</div>

<div class="class_s1PM">

Now when loop begins it will prints the print statement as well as it
increment the value of variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> by
<span class="class_s4UC">1</span> . After that, the second iteration
started in which the value of variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span>
is updated to <span class="class_s4UC">2</span> . Again it will check
the condition. As <span class="class_s4UC">2</span> is also less than
<span class="class_s4UC">5,</span> which satisfied the condition and
print the statement. After printing it, values updated to <span
class="class_s4UC">3</span> and so on.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now, when value of <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> becomes <span
class="class_s4UC">6</span> , the while loop will check the <span
id="text00011.html#page_128"></span> condition. As condition is not
satisfied so loop will terminate.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now the above code gives the output as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s2BK-0">

![](Image00328.jpg){.class_s2BK-1}

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00329.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

condition, as long as </span> <span class="class_s4UM">x</span> <span
class="class_s4UN"> doesn't equal 99, display </span> <span
class="class_s4UM">x</span> <span class="class_s4UN">, then increment it
by 1 using the concise way to increment.</span>

</div>

loop is True

In the following block, we have an example of break statement in while
loop

![](Image00331.jpg){.class_s28P-0}

integer value <span class="class_s4UC">3.</span>

loop.</span>

In while loop, the continue statement can stop the specific iteration,
and again continue with next iterations.

of <span class="class_s4UC">break()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Let’s have a look to the given example. Now if we want a loop to print

 ![](Image00334.jpg){.class_s2CS}

class="class_s4UE">Spaghetti Bolognese</span> <span
class="class_s4VV">.</span> <span id="text00011.html#page_131"></span>

may be greater than 10. So in these types of cases we set a flag.

<span class="class_s4UC">favourite\_foods</span> <span

full stop (.), then flag will set to <span

Otherwise, it will add another input to the list favourite foods

Chapter 12 : Changing Case

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Python is case sensitive which means that if we take input from user and
we don’t define the user to use capital letter or small letter. For
example,

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If the person is applying to some driving job and he has to answer the
following question,

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00339.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here the user type yes, as yes is not to equals to YES in python so, it
will not print “Congratulations!”

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If we want to change the case of string data we can use the following
built\_in functions:

</div>

-   upper()
-   lower()
-   title()

<div id="text00012.html#a4RU" class="heading_sFV">

12.1 The function upper

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In the following, we set a condition that if variable <span
class="class_s4UC">Question</span> equals to <span
class="class_s4UC">yes</span> than it must print “Congratulation!”. Here
we use function <span class="class_s4UC">upper().</span> It basically
returns the uppercased string from the given string. And if there is no
lowercased character it will reture the original.
![](Image00340.jpg){.class_s2E6}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Again, the user gives the input <span class="class_s4UC">yes</span> ,
the upper fuction will convert into <span class="class_s4UC">YES</span>
.So YES equals to YES staisfy the condition will print <span
id="text00012.html#page_134"></span> “Congratulations!”.

</div>

<div id="text00012.html#a4RV" class="heading_sFV">

12.2 The function lower

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Similarly, we can use <span class="class_s4UC">lower()</span> function.
Here we assigned <span class="class_s4UC">CHAIR</span> to the variable
<span class="class_s4UC">noun</span> . We convert it as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s27W-1">

![](Image00341.jpg){.class_s27W-0}

</div>

<div id="text00012.html#a4RW" class="heading_s1K0">

12.3 The function title

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

This function will convert first letter of each word to upper case and
remaining to the lower case. Here we want to change first alphabet of
each word to upper case so we simply use function <span
class="class_s4UC">title(). </span>

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00342.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4RX" class="heading_sDR">

Chapter 13 : Functions

</div>

<div class="class_s2EY">

In python, the function is the way to achieve two things: Modularity and
Reusability. Let’s get familiar with these two:

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

<span class="class_s4UE">1)Modularity</span> : It means that we are
breaking our programme into smaller and modular chunks. As our programme
is not always simple but grows larger and larger, the function makes it
organized and <span class="class_s4UF">practicable.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

<span class="class_s4UE">2)Reusability:</span> As word says it can be
use again and again. So if we write multiple lines of code, we can give
these lines a name and use these lines by just calling the name of
function rather than writing the whole block of code again.

</div>

<div class="class_s2F4-1">

![](Image00343.jpg){.class_s2F4-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s1PM">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax:</span> We use the keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">def</span> (for define) after that we will use
function name with two parentheses <span class="class_s4UE">()</span> .
We can also place input parameters or arguments within these parentheses
or can also define parameters inside these parentheses followed by colon
<span class="class_s4UE">(:)</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sPS">

def function\_name():

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_136" class="class_s2FA-0">

![](Image00344.jpg){.class_s2FA-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we define two variables <span class="class_s4UC">x</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">y.</span> We assign the value <span
class="class_s4UC">5</span> to the variable <span
class="class_s4UC">x</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">10</span> to
the variable <span class="class_s4UC">y</span> . Also we have another
variable <span class="class_s4UC">c</span> which add the values from
<span class="class_s4UC">x</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">y</span>
and store it as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s1NS-0">

![](Image00345.jpg){.class_s1NS-1}

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

We get the integer value <span class="class_s4UC">15</span> as an
output. In the following topic, we will discuss that how we can do this
by using functions.

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4RY" class="heading_sFV">

13.1 Parameter less function

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Function with no parameters within the parentheses of function
definition.

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4RZ" class="heading_s81">

13.1.1 User-defined functions

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The function in which variables take the value from the user is called
User-defined functions.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here, we again define two variables <span class="class_s4UC">x</span>
and <span class="class_s4UC">y</span> <span
id="text00013.html#page_137"></span> . Both variables take input from
the user and convert the string data type to the integer data type.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

And at last <span class="class_s4UC">print()</span> function will add
these two variables and print their value.

</div>

<div class="class_s270-1">

![](Image00346.jpg){.class_s270-0}

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00347.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Suppose, we assigned the values <span class="class_s4UC">5</span> and
<span class="class_s4UC">10</span> to the variables <span
class="class_s4UC">x</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">y</span> then
it will print <span class="class_s4UC">15</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now if we want again to do this task we have to write it all over again.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We can do it again thousands times easily just by turning this code into
function.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we defines the function named <span class="class_s4UC">add</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00348.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s1WU">

By executing this block no operation will be performed. Function <span
id="text00013.html#page_138"></span> will not executes itself but remain
in silent mode and didn’t do anything until the function is called.

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00349.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

For example, we have <span class="class_s4UC">print()</span> statement
before and after the function.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

![](Image00350.jpg){.class_s2GC} By executing the following block we get
output i-e <span class="class_s4UC">hye</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">bye</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

But it didn’t execute the function. It will execute only when it is
called.\
 

</div>

<div class="class_s2GH-1">

![](Image00351.jpg){.class_s2GH-0}

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_139" class="class_s79">

<div id="text00013.html#a4S0" class="heading_s2GW">

13.2 Parameterise function

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Function with parameters within the parentheses of function definition.

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4S1" class="heading_s81">

13.2.1 Passing information positional argument

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We learned that, how to make a function and code it. Suppose you made a
function to subtract two values named the function as <span
class="class_s4UC">subtract.</span> So whenever you call it by writing a
<span class="class_s4UC">subtract()</span> <span
id="text00013.html#page_140"></span> it will execute the function
robotically.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now again look at this,

</div>

<div class="class_sPS">

subtract()

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we don’t want these parentheses to be empty. We can put some
information inside it. So whenever it executes, use these information
.For example, we can write it as

</div>

<div class="class_sPS">

subtract(10,5)

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now function will take these two values and subtract them. These values
are called <span class="class_s4UE">arguments</span> . The arguments
inside parentheses and separated by comma.

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00354.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax:</span> First we have to write variables
inside the function definition. These variables inside parentheses
separated by comma <span class="class_s4UE">(,)</span> .We called these
variables as parameters.

</div>

<div class="class_s2HA">

<span class="class_s4V5">def function\_name(parameter\_1, parameter\_2
):</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s2EY">

For example,

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

![](Image00355.jpg){.class_s2HG} In the function <span
class="class_s4UC">subtract () a</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">b</span> are the parameters.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we call the function by passing the values <span
class="class_s4UC">10</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">5</span> <span
id="text00013.html#page_141"></span> .And it will give the value of
<span class="class_s4UC">5</span> after subtracting them

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00356.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Note that the value <span class="class_s4UC">5</span> will assigned to
the variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">10</span> to the variable <span
class="class_s4UC">b</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s1NS-0">

![](Image00357.jpg){.class_s1NS-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now if we give arguments <span class="class_s4UC">1.5</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">5</span> then the result will be,

</div>

<div class="class_s28P-1">

![](Image00358.jpg){.class_s28P-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As value <span class="class_s4UC">1.5</span> is assigned to <span
class="class_s4UC">a</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">5</span> to
<span class="class_s4UC">b</span> . As it subtract <span
class="class_s4UC">5</span> from <span class="class_s4UC">1.5</span> i-e
1.5-5=-3.5

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As, it display float value with the negative sign.

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

Here is another example,

</div>

<div class="class_s270-1">

![](Image00359.jpg){.class_s270-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now we call the function by passing the string.

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_142" class="class_s1KR-0">

![](Image00360.jpg){.class_s1KR-1}

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

![](Image00361.jpg){.class_s2JB} ![](Image00016.jpg){.class_sD7} <span
class="class_s4UE">Remember:</span> If we pass argument greater or less
then the parameter, we will get an error. So the number of argument must
be equal to the number the parameters.

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

We call a function by passing the arguments to the function. They
matched according to their position in the function call. In the
following, we have a function <span class="class_s4UC">fullname</span>
having three parameters: <span class="class_s4UC">first, Middle</span>
and <span class="class_s4UC">last,</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s1NS-0">

![](Image00362.jpg){.class_s1NS-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here string <span class="class_s4UC">Mohammad</span> assigned to the
<span class="class_s4UC">first</span> , <span
class="class_s4UC">Hamza</span> assigned to <span
class="class_s4UC">middle</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Iqbal</span> assigned to the <span
class="class_s4UC">last.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_143" class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00363.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s2JP">

13.2.2 Passing information keyword argument

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Another way of calling the function is by passing the argument as well
as the parameter. By this method, position does not matter anymore but
value (argument) will assigned to the matching variable in the function
parameter.

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00364.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Let’s discuss the above example again, in which function <span
class="class_s4UC">fullname</span> having three parameters: <span
class="class_s4UC">first, Middle</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">last</span> . If we disturb the sequence, we will get
different name. For example, if we pass middle name first and last name
in the middle we will get, ![](Image00365.jpg){.class_s2JZ}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now we will call the function again by passing the argument attach with
the parameter. For example, ![](Image00366.jpg){.class_s2K4}

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_144" class="class_sPN">

Note that there is no sequence in the arguments but we get the output
orderly .Each value is assigned to their parameter by matching the
keyword attached to it.

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

Middle value is assigned to the middle parameter although we pass this
argument first but sequence does not matter anymore. Similarly, first
value assigned to <span class="class_s4UC">first</span> parameter and
value last to <span class="class_s4UC">last</span> parameter.

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

Now if we don’t want to give all the keyword argument but only few one
then we can write that parameter in the last. The Keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">argument</span> always follows the positional
argument. It can be written as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s270-1">

![](Image00367.jpg){.class_s270-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now, if we pass the last keyword argument first, we will get an error as
follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s270-1">

![](Image00368.jpg){.class_s270-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Also, if we do not know that how many arguments can a function take or
how many arguments can a user pass? Then we will use <span
class="class_s4UE">args</span>

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4S2" class="heading_s11T">

13.2.3 Args

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

By this method, we can call a function by passing a various number of
arguments. It is used to pass a non-keyword, variable-length argument
list.

</div>

<div class="class_s1PM">

It uses the symbol <span class="class_s4UE">(\*)</span> <span
id="text00013.html#page_145"></span> . Using this, the variable becomes
iterable.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

For example, if the user wants to pass more than one argument in the
given parameter then it use <span class="class_s4UE">\*</span> with the
parameter. This parameter can store a lot of values inside it. As we
read it before that a variable containing more values is known as <span
class="class_s4UE">tuple.</span> So, when we get this parameter we see
values store in the tuple.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We can write it as follows:

</div>

<div class="class_s2KS">

<div class="class_s2KP">

<span class="class_s4V5">def fun(\*parameter)</span>

</div>

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As this is known as optional number depends upon the user.

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

Here we have example of ordering pizza. As the function <span
class="class_s4UC">pizza\_order</span> have three main parameters i-e
<span class="class_s4UE">size flavour</span> and <span
class="class_s4UE">toppings</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

![](Image00369.jpg){.class_sRG}

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

Now the restaurateur will take the order from customer by passing the
arguments to the function like the following<span
class="class_s4UF">,</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00370.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now it prints the above message as an output. But, if the customer wants
more than one topping?

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We use <span class="class_s4UE">\*</span> operation with the parameter
topping.  Now <span class="class_s4UC">\*toppings</span> become the
parameter deals with the arbitrary arguments. It can <span
id="text00013.html#page_146"></span> written as,

</div>

<div class="class_s1KR-0">

![](Image00371.jpg){.class_s1KR-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

</div>

<div class="class_s28P-1">

![](Image00372.jpg){.class_s28P-0}

tuple.

</div>

<div class="class_s1NS-0">

![](Image00373.jpg){.class_s1NS-1}

<div id="text00013.html#a4S3" class="heading_s11T">

13.2.4 Default value parameter

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We see that we call the parameterised function by passing the arguments.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If a user does not provide any arguments then type error will occur. To
avoid any non deterministic behaviour python allows us to set default
values in it. For example, we can set some default values as follows,

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_147" class="class_s2MS-0">

![](Image00374.jpg){.class_s2MS-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As parameter <span class="class_s4UC">x</span> having default value of
<span class="class_s4UC">2</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">y</span>
having value of <span class="class_s4UC">3</span> .Now we call it
without passing the arguments so the output will be,

</div>

<div class="class_s2MX-1">

![](Image00375.jpg){.class_s2MX-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As the function uses it default values and print something. If the user
just passes the argument <span class="class_s4UC">y</span> then we will
get,

</div>

<div class="class_s2MS-0">

![](Image00376.jpg){.class_s2MS-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As the user do not pass <span class="class_s4UC">x</span> so the
function use default value of <span class="class_s4UC">x</span> but
update the value of <span class="class_s4UC">y</span> with <span
class="class_s4UC">7</span> so it prints <span
class="class_s4UC">9.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s2N4">

Looking again to the previous example of the function <span
class="class_s4UC">fullname</span> . This function takes three arguments
and assigned to their respective parameters. Let’s suppose a person have
no middle name. Now we can set default value of the middle name. So if
the user doesn’t enters its middle name the default value will print.

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_148" class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00377.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00378.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we put default value of space in argument middle. So when user
don’t have middle name the function will use space bar.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now user calls the function by passing its name consist of first name
and last name as follows:

</div>

<div class="class_s1NS-0">

![](Image00379.jpg){.class_s1NS-1}

<div id="text00013.html#a4S4" class="heading_s2CJ">

13.2.5 Passing information back from them

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_149" class="class_s79">

When we call a function then function will perform the task given to it.
The function receives values, processes it and prints it.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

For example, we have a function <span class="class_s4UC">add</span> .Now
we call this function by passing the arguments and the function prints
integer <span class="class_s4UC">18</span> by processing it as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00380.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now, we want to do some operations with the result of the function but
unfortunately, we cannot do it because the result still present inside
the body of the function. As, the value of <span
class="class_s4UC">c</span> print on screen but it is not possible for
us to use it

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

Now to take out this value we use keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">return().</span> These returned values can be assign,
reuse and modify then.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We write return inside the body of function. We can code it as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s270-1">

![](Image00381.jpg){.class_s270-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now this returned the value inside the variable <span
class="class_s4UC">c</span> to the variable result which is outside the
body.

</div>

-   First we call the function by passing arguments.
-   The values are assigned to the variable <span
    class="class_s4UC">x</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">y</span> .
-   The result of adding these values is assigned to the variable <span
    class="class_s4UC">c</span> <span
    id="text00013.html#page_150"></span> .
-   Keyword return will give value of <span class="class_s4UC">c</span>
    to the variable <span class="class_s4UC">result</span> outside the
    function body.

<div class="class_s2P6-1">

![](Image00382.jpg){.class_s2P6-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We will re-utilize this value anytime. For example,

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00383.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We multiplied result with <span class="class_s4UC">2</span> then we get
integer value <span class="class_s4UC">36</span> .i-e as result having
value of <span class="class_s4UC">36</span> .

</div>

-   Integer
-   Any user defined input.

</div>

    from user and at last it return message.
-   Now we call the function by passing arguments.

<div class="class_s2R7">

Remember that the number of arguments must be equal to the

</div>

<div class="class_s2R9">

number of parameters.

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

<span id="text00013.html#page_152"></span> York then user can call

Return must be the last line of execution in the function.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If we want to print this message we can take this statement out of the
body by removing the indentation.

</div>

<div class="class_s2RW">

The statement return \[expression\] exits a function, optionally passing
back an expression to the caller. A return statement with no arguments
is the same as return <span class="class_s4UE">None.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4S6" class="heading_sJ6">

13.3 Using function as variables

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_153" class="class_s79">

Basically, the main purpose of function is that it can be use as the
variables. This is done by calling the function in the expression.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Here we have two different functions <span class="class_s4UC">mul</span>
and <span class="class_s4UC">div.</span> These functions having
parameters <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">b</span> .We can assign different values to the
argument of two functions.

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00391.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now, we call these functions inside the new variable <span
class="class_s4UC">c</span> . It will perform addition and assign the
result to the variable <span class="class_s4UC">c.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00392.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

-   First, the function <span class="class_s4UC">div</span> call and
    assign arguments <span class="class_s4UC">6</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">3</span> to parameters <span
    class="class_s4UC">a</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">b</span> .
-   Now it divides <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> by <span
    class="class_s4UC">b</span> and returns the result to <span
    class="class_s4UC">div(6,3)</span>
-   Similarly, second function called by passing the arguments <span
    class="class_s4UC">5</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">10</span>
    to the variable <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">b</span> .
-   Now values of <span class="class_s4UC">a</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">b</span> will updated from <span
    class="class_s4UC">6</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">3</span> to
    <span class="class_s4UC">5</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">10</span>

<div class="class_s2SF-1">

![](Image00393.jpg){.class_s2SF-0}

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_154" class="class_s79">

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00394.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

![](Image00395.jpg){.class_sRG}

<div id="text00013.html#a4S8" class="heading_s11T">

13.3.1 Local and global variables

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Let’s discuss two types of variable used in the functions.

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4W1" class="heading_s22Z">

13.3.1.1 Local variable

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Local variables are the variables, which defines inside the body of the
function.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The scope is only inside the function as it means that they are
recognized locally. They are not accessible outside the function.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We have a function <span class="class_s4UC">yesterday</span> in the
following code,

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00396.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

Look there is a variable <span class="class_s4UC">weather</span> inside
the function body. So it is local variable .String <span
class="class_s4UC">Sunny</span> is stored in this local variable. When
we call the function <span class="class_s4UC">yesterday</span> we get
the following output,

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_155" class="class_s1MP-1">

![](Image00397.jpg){.class_s1MP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As we studied that local variable are not able to access from outside
the body. So, if want to access the local variable <span
class="class_s4UC">weather</span> it will produce an error.

</div>

<div class="class_s2T9-0">

![](Image00398.jpg){.class_s2T9-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

It says that the variable <span class="class_s4UE">weather</span> is not
defined.

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4VH" class="heading_s2TC">

13.3.1.2 Global variable

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

<span class="class_s4UE">Global variables</span> are the variables,
which defines outside the body of the function.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Global scope is like global fame as these can be accessed and modify
from inside as well outside the function.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Again, we have the function <span class="class_s4UC">today</span> . Now
we have a variable <span class="class_s4UC">weather2</span> in which
string <span class="class_s4UC">Rainy</span> is stored. The variable
<span class="class_s4UC">weather2</span> is outside the function so it
is global variable. Inside the function there is print statement, which
prints the value of a global variable successfully.

</div>

<div class="class_s1MP-1">

![](Image00399.jpg){.class_s1MP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If we call the function <span class="class_s4UC">today</span> , it will
print the following message,

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#page_156" class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00400.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now as <span class="class_s4UC">weather2</span> is global variable so it
should be accessible from outside the body of function like,

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

![](Image00401.jpg){.class_s2TW} Great! it prints the string value
stored in it.

</div>

<div id="text00013.html#a4S9" class="heading_s1K0">

13.4 Function within function

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Till now we have learnt how to make the function. Now we can also call
the function within the other function.

</div>

-   Suppose we have a function name <span
    class="class_s4UC">commission\_calculator</span> in which we set
    different conditions. We have given parameter <span
    class="class_s4UC">sales</span> to the function <span
    class="class_s4UC">commission\_calculator</span> .
-   We use <span class="class_s4UE">if statement</span> for
    decision making. It will run throughout the body and check
    the condition. It returns when the condition is true.
-   Another function is <span
    class="class_s4UC">salary\_calculator.</span> This function has two
    parameters i-e <span class="class_s4UC">basic</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">sales</span> .
-   Inside the function we have a variable <span
    class="class_s4UC">grossSalary</span> which adds two parameters i-e
    <span class="class_s4UC">basic</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">sales</span> (from the first function <span
    class="class_s4UC">commission\_calculator)</span> . It can code as
    follows,

<div id="text00013.html#page_157" class="class_s2AG-0">

![](Image00402.jpg){.class_s2AG-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now we have to call the main function <span
class="class_s4UC">salary\_calculator</span> by passing the arguments.
Here the data type of both arguments will be integer. We call the
function by passing the values <span class="class_s4UC">500</span> as
<span class="class_s4UC">basic</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">55</span> as <span class="class_s4UC">sales</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s2UB-1">

![](Image00403.jpg){.class_s2UB-0}

</div>

-   First, by calling the function it assigned the values of arguments
    in their parameter.
-   The integer <span class="class_s4UC">500</span> assigned to
    parameter basic and integer <span class="class_s4UC">55</span>
    assigned to parameter s<span class="class_s4UC">ales</span> . Sales
    called in the function <span
    class="class_s4UC">commission\_calcutor.</span>
-   Now <span class="class_s4UC">commission\_calculator</span> check
    all condition. As, sales is not greater than <span
    class="class_s4UC">100</span> so it check next condition. The next
    condition says that the sale must be greater than <span
    class="class_s4UC">50</span> as sales equals to <span
    class="class_s4UC">55</span> which is greater than <span
    class="class_s4UC">50</span> so condition is true.
-   Then, it returned the value by multiplying sales with <span
    class="class_s4UC">50 i-e 50\*50 equals to 2750</span>
-   The variable <span class="class_s4UC">grossSalary</span> adds basic
    and sales i-e 500+2750 equals to 3250.
-   Then print the following output,<span
    id="text00013.html#page_158"></span>

<div class="class_s2UM">

“Your gross salary is 3250”

</div>

<span class="class_s4UV-0">Task:</span> <span class="class_s4US">Code a
function</span> <span class="class_s4UT">full\_name</span> <span
class="class_s4US">having two parameters (first\_name and last\_name).
Concatenate</span> <span class="class_s4UT">first\_name</span> <span
class="class_s4US">and</span> <span class="class_s4UT">last\_name</span>
<span class="class_s4US">and assigns the result to a variable</span>
<span class="class_s4UT">x,</span> <span class="class_s4US">and passes
the result back to the calling code.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SA" class="heading_sDR">

Chapter 14 : Classes

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SB" class="heading_s1K0">

14.1 Introduction

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As Python is an object oriented programming language. It means all the
code in python is implemented using special construct called <span
class="class_s4UE">class</span> <span class="class_s4UC">.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The first concept of object oriented programming language is classes.

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

A class is defined as a model, blueprint(map) of anything or it is also
defined as something that can be followed to create objects and
instances.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In Python, <span class="class_s4UE">classes</span> are template.
Template means that we can create similar things by using that template.
For example, when someone conduct a survey of the questionnaire sort, he
hands you a survey form having some listed questions in it.<span
class="class_s4VN"> </span> Surveyor asked Surveye, to answer all the
questions written in the form. <span class="class_s4V5">Why doesn’t the
surveyor gives you a blank sheet and asked to write your thoughts on
that specific topic?</span> As the survey team wants only specific
information about that subject from you. The form is just like a
template that makes things easier for both surveyor and the surveyee. It
organized information so that the result is easily concluded from that
specific set of information.

</div>

<div class="class_sPN">

The advantage of using classes is to keep related things together.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_160" class="class_s2V5-0">

![](Image00404.jpg){.class_s2V5-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax</span> : Python use keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">class</span> to define a class. And write name of
class with parenthesis and colon <span class="class_s4UE">(:)</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s2V8">

class Survey() :

</div>

<div class="class_s2VA">

\#body of class

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

After colon body of a class starts. Now we might think that what class
holds inside its body? So a class can hold two things:

</div>

-   A class may hold attributes
-   A class may hold behaviours

<div class="class_s79">

In programming, attributes means <span
class="class_s4UE">variables</span> and behaviours means <span
class="class_s4UE">functions</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We will discuss both variable and function within the class one by one

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Looking to the example of class. Let’s talk about some real example such
as car. We all are familiar with common attributes of a car such as
color of a car, size of a car, model of a car or setting capacity of a
car. Similarly, we also notice some behaviours of a car which includes
movement of a car, acceleration of a car, deceleration of a car or
steering speed of a car. These are called functions of class car.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we write a class named <span class="class_s4UC">Car</span> ,

</div>

<div class="class_s2VA">

class Car() <span id="text00014.html#page_161"></span> :

</div>

<div class="class_s2VN">

\#body of class

</div>

<div class="class_s2VR">

\#attributes and behaviours

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00405.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s2VW">

Here the car company can store information of different cars but all the
information is to be structured in the same way.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SC" class="heading_sBN">

14.2 Variable in the class

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In class first we have to define the attributes/variables. Those
attributes must be in object of that specific class.

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

For that we make a function by using,

</div>

-   keyword <span class="class_s4UE">def</span> <span
    class="class_s4V5">.</span>
-   After that we type underscore two time <span
    class="class_s4UE">(\_\_)</span>
-   Then type keyword <span class="class_s4UE">init</span>
-   Again, type two times underscore <span
    class="class_s4UE">(\_\_)</span>
-   Opening the parentheses, then write keyword <span
    class="class_s4UE">self</span> as first parameter
-   After that we can write attributes of that class
-   End the line with closing parentheses and colon <span
    class="class_s4UE">(:)</span>

<div class="class_s2PN">

For example,

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_162" class="class_s2WD-1">

![](Image00406.jpg){.class_s2WD-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s2WF">

</div>

<div class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00407.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

Here we have a class <span class="class_s4UE">Car().</span> Now we have
to define the attribute of class <span class="class_s4UC">Car</span> i-e
color.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

After that we must have a variable having same value as attributes

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00408.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Note that second line is intended because of colon in the end of first
line which means second line is in the body of a class.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Inside the function body, we write variables. Here we declare a variable
<span class="class_s4UC">self.car\_color</span> in which we save the
value of the attribute <span class="class_s4UC">color</span> .

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_163" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00409.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

line.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00410.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

We can also defined attributes of a class before as the following

</div>

<div class="class_s2X3">

class Car() :

</div>

</div>

def\_\_init\_\_(self,attribute):

</div>

</div>

self.attribute=attribute

<div id="text00014.html#a4SD" class="heading_sBN">

14.3 Objects

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Almost everything in Python is an object with its properties and
methods.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Objects are instances of classes. All objects follow the specific class.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We defined the class above named it as <span
class="class_s4UC">Car().</span> By defining it, means we only defined
the description of object.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00411.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Object are made following its class, means that object belongs to a
class. The instances must have been following the requirements set by
the class.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_165" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00412.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

First we write name of object, then assignment operator <span
class="class_s4UE">(=)</span> , then name of a class and parenthesis
<span class="class_s4UE">().</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s2XU">

object1 = Class()

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Similarly, for creating <span class="class_s4UC">object 2</span> we can
write the following,

</div>

<div class="class_s2XU">

object2 = Class()

</div>

<div class="heading_s81">

<div id="text00014.html#toc116_">

![](Image00413.jpg){.class_s2Y0}

</div>

</div>

<div class="class_s304">

attributes of a class i-e color of a car ,make of a car and model of a

</div>

    class="class_s4UC">Car\_1, Car\_2</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">Car\_3</span>
-   Then write dot (<span class="class_s4UE">.</span> )
-   At last write name of attribute which we want to display.

<div class="class_s32B">

indentifier.attribute

</div>

14.3.5 Adding an attribute value to a class

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As we have a class <span class="class_s4UC">car()</span> having
attributes <span class="class_s4UC">color, make, model</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">price</span> . Also we have three instances <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_1</span> ,<span class="class_s4UC">Car\_2</span>
and <span class="class_s4UC">Car\_3</span> . Now we want to add a new
attribute <span class="class_s4UC">GPS\_Navigation\_System</span> to the
instance <span class="class_s4UC">Car\_1.</span> We can add it by using
function <span class="class_s4UC">setattr()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In this function, first we pass instance name then name of the attribute
and at last, value of that attribute. We can write it as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sWS-1">

![](Image00441.jpg){.class_sWS-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00442.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now, we access that attribute with the function <span
class="class_s4UC">getattr().</span> In this <span
id="text00014.html#page_178"></span> function first we pass the instance
name than the name of attribute as in the following code,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00443.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00444.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The value of the attribute is only added to the instance <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_1.</span> If we want to get this attribute for
other instance like <span class="class_s4UC">Car\_2</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_3</span> it will shows us an error.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00445.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

14.3.6 Deleting an attribute value of a class

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We can also delete any specific attribute from the instance by using
function <span class="class_s4UC">delattr()</span> . First we have to
pass instance name and then the attribute name which we have to delete.
Now we want to delete the attribute price from instance Car\_1. We can
write the code as follows,

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_179" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00446.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

It removes the attribute price from instance <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_1</span> but still it is present in other
instances <span class="class_s4UC">Car\_2</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_3</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SR" class="heading_s81">

14.3.7 Checking an attribute value of a class

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

To check the attribute weather it is present in the instance or not, we
simply use the function <span class="class_s4UC">hasattr()</span> . This
function also needs the instance name and the attribute name which have
to be check. Now we want to see that the attribute <span
class="class_s4UC">GPS\_Naviagtion\_System</span> is present in the
instance <span class="class_s4UC">Car\_1</span> so we write the
following code,

</div>

<div class="class_sMA-0">

![](Image00447.jpg){.class_sMA-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

It returns <span class="class_s4UE">True</span> . As the instance <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_2</span> doesn’t has this attribute so when we
check for <span class="class_s4UC">Car\_2</span> it would returns <span
class="class_s4UE">False.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00448.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SS" class="heading_s81">

14.3.8 Changing an attribute value of a class

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

First write name of the instance followed by dot(.). Then write the
attribute which we want to update. And then assign new value to it by
writing new value after assignment operator,

</div>

<div class="class_s340">

instance\_name.attribute=new\_value

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Again recalling the previous example, we defined a class <span
class="class_s4UC">Car()</span> having three instances <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_1, Car\_2</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_3.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_180" class="class_s7V">

Also, we know that we can easily get all the information out of these
instances .Here we get the value for attribute <span
class="class_s4UC">color</span> of instance <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_1</span> by writing the following code,
![](Image00449.jpg){.class_s346}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we want to change the color for instance <span
class="class_s4UC">Car\_1</span> from <span
class="class_s4UC">Yellow</span> to <span
class="class_s4UC">Black</span> we can write it as follows

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00450.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We can verify it by calling the attribute through instance. As,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00451.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Great! Value updated.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SU" class="heading_sBN">

14.4 Class Inheritance

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We can create more classes by using original class instead of starting
from scratch, by using the concept of Inheritance. Inheritance is a
method of creating new classes by using the details of existing class
without changing it.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now here we have two types of classes,

</div>

-   <span class="class_s4UE">Original class:</span> The original or
    existing class is called base class.
-   <span class="class_s4UE">New class:</span> The class which inherits
    the property of the base class is called derived class.

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00470.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We have following types of Inheritance:

</div>

-   Single Inheritance
-   Multiple Inheritance
-   <div id="text00014.html#page_186">

    </div>

    Multi level Inheritance
-   Hierarchical Inheritance
-   Hybrid Inheritance

<div class="class_sUE">

We will discuss each one by one.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SV" class="heading_s37W">

14.4.1 Single Inheritance

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Single Inheritance means that <span class="class_s4UE">a derived
class</span> inherits the method and attributes from single base class.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax:</span> First, we have to write the base
class and after that we define derived class. We use keyword class to
define both classes,

</div>

<div class="class_s380">

class Base\_Class:

</div>

<div class="class_s382">

body of base class

</div>

<div class="class_s380">

class Dervied\_Class(Base\_Class):

</div>

<div class="class_s385">

body of derived class

</div>

<div class="class_s387">

In the following diagram, Classes are represented as boxes. The
inheritance relationship is represented by an arrow from base class
pointing to the derived class,

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_187" class="class_s38B-0">

![](Image00471.jpg){.class_s38B-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let’s do an example of Inheritance. Recalling the above example of class
<span class="class_s4UC">Car</span> (). Here we have super class <span
class="class_s4UC">Vehicle()</span> and a sub class <span
class="class_s4UC">Car()</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

First, we define the super class <span
class="class_s4UC">Vehical()</span> as
follows,![](Image00472.jpg){.class_s38H}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In the super class <span class="class_s4UC">Vehicle(),</span> we
instantiate a constructor with <span class="class_s4UC">make</span> and
<span class="class_s4UC">color</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

After super class, we define the sub class <span
class="class_s4UC">Car().</span> In the parentheses we put the name of
the parent class i-e <span class="class_s4UC">Vehicle.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We write the code for sub class as follows,

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_188" class="class_sNV-1">

![](Image00473.jpg){.class_sNV-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UY">Here, we call the constructor from the sub
class Car using</span> <span class="class_s4UZ">super().</span> <span
class="class_s4UY">Also we created a </span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">get\_description</span> <span
class="class_s4UY"> method which is returning </span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">self.model</span> <span class="class_s4UY">from sub
class. Also this method is returning</span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">self.make, self.color</span> <span
class="class_s4UY"> from the super class</span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">Vehicle().</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00474.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UY">Now, we define instance</span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">c</span> <span class="class_s4UY">for sub
class</span> <span class="class_s4UZ">Car().</span> <span
class="class_s4UY">As the string values matches with the attribute of
class,</span> ![](Image00475.jpg){.class_s390}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UY">Here the string value</span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">Ford</span> <span class="class_s4UY">assigned
to</span> <span class="class_s4UZ">make, Mustang</span> <span
class="class_s4UY">assigned to</span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">model</span> <span class="class_s4UY">and</span>
<span class="class_s4UZ">Yellow</span> <span class="class_s4UY">assigned
to</span> <span class="class_s4UZ">color.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_189" class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UY">Note that above block have two print
statements. In the first print statement we call the method</span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">get\_description</span> <span class="class_s4UY">from
the sub class</span> <span class="class_s4UZ">Car().</span> <span
class="class_s4UY">And in the second print statement we call the
method</span> <span class="class_s4UZ">get\_make</span> <span
class="class_s4UY">from the super</span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">class()</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SW" class="heading_s81">

14.4.2 Multiple Inheritance

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In Inheritance we see that a derived class <span
class="class_s4UY">inherits the method and attributes from base class.
If the derived class inherits the property from multiple base classes
then it is known as multiple inheritance.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s396">

This method allows us to use the properties from multiple base classes
in a derived or child class.

</div>

<div class="class_s398">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s385">

class Base\_Class\_1:

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

body of base class

</div>

<div class="class_s39D">

class Base\_Class\_2:

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

body of base class

</div>

<div class="class_s39D">

class Dervied\_Class(Base\_Class\_1,Base\_Class\_2):

</div>

<div class="class_s12X">

body of derived class

</div>

<div class="class_s12J">

In the following diagram, the inheritance relationship is represented by
an arrow from two base classes pointing to the same derived class.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_190" class="class_s39N-0">

![](Image00476.jpg){.class_s39N-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UY">Recalling the above example, where we have a
super class</span> <span class="class_s4UC">Vehicle()</span> having a
sub class <span class="class_s4UC">Car().</span> Now we do the same
example with the concept of multiple inheritance. Here we have super
class having attribute <span class="class_s4UC">make</span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sNV-1">

![](Image00477.jpg){.class_sNV-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we add another super class <span class="class_s4UC">Cost()</span>
having attribute <span class="class_s4UC">cost,</span> as in the
following,

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_191" class="class_sWS-1">

![](Image00478.jpg){.class_sWS-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

So here we have sub class <span class="class_s4UC">Car</span> . It works
similar to the inheritance example discussed previous. <span
class="class_s4UY">We have created a </span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">get\_description</span> <span
class="class_s4UY">method which is returning </span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">self.model</span> <span class="class_s4UY">from sub
class. Also this method is returning</span> <span
class="class_s4UZ">self.make</span> <span class="class_s4UY">and</span>
<span class="class_s4UZ">self.cost</span> <span class="class_s4UY">from
the super classes</span> <span class="class_s4UZ">Vehicle()</span> <span
class="class_s4UY">and</span> <span class="class_s4UZ">Cost()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s3A2-1">

![](Image00479.jpg){.class_s3A2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Note that,

</div>

-   We want to inherit the properties of both super classes <span
    class="class_s4UC">Vehicle</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">Cost</span> . So, we have to write the name of
    super class inside the parenthesis of sub class.
-   We call the attribute in the constructor of sub class <span
    class="class_s4UC">Car</span> by using another method i-e the name
    of super class,

<div class="class_s3A9">

<span class="class_s4V5">Vehicle.\_\_init\_\_(self,make)</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s3AB">

Cost.\_\_init\_\_(self,cost)

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we define instances <span class="class_s4UC">c</span> of sub class
<span class="class_s4UC">Car</span> <span
id="text00014.html#page_192"></span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00480.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The values match with the attributes. Here string value <span
class="class_s4UC">Ford</span> matches with <span
class="class_s4UC">self.make,</span> <span
class="class_s4UC">Mustang</span> matches with <span
class="class_s4UC">self.model</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">\$35630</span> matches with the attribute <span
class="class_s4UC">cost.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SX" class="heading_s81">

14.4.3 Multilevel Inheritance

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In multilevel inheritance, we have one base class, one derived class and
sub derived class which means that the feature of base class and derived
class is further inherited by another derived class.

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Snytax:

</div>

<div class="class_s39D">

class Base\_Class:

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

body of base class

</div>

<div class="class_s39D">

class Derived\_Class(Base\_Class):

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

body of derived class

</div>

<div class="class_s39D">

class Dervied\_Class\_2(Derived\_Class):

</div>

<div class="class_s12X">

body of derived class

</div>

<div class="class_s12J">

In the following diagram, Classes are represented as boxes. The
inheritance relationship is represented by an arrow from the base class
pointing to the derived class. And another, derived class is inherited
from derived class. 

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_193" class="class_s3AY-0">

![](Image00481.jpg){.class_s3AY-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

This type of Inheritance works same as relationship between child and
grandfather. Let’s do an example. We can write the following code to
define a base class named <span class="class_s4UC">Grandfather()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00482.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Also we derived a class from a base class named <span
class="class_s4UC">Father().</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_194" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00483.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00484.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_sEY">

Now we define another class which is further derived from class <span
class="class_s4UC">Father()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00485.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we define instances <span class="class_s4UC">s</span> for the class
<span class="class_s4UC">Son().</span> First we are assigning string
values <span class="class_s4UC">Graham</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">John</span> to the variables <span
class="class_s4UC">grandfathername</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">fathername</span> . Then we are calling method parent
from the derived class <span class="class_s4UC">Son().</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_195" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00486.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

By running above code we get the following output,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00487.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UM">Task:</span> <span class="class_s4UN">Define a
class</span> <span class="class_s4VU">student()</span> <span
class="class_s4UN">with one attribute</span> <span
class="class_s4VU">major</span> <span class="class_s4UN">and one method.
The method displays the attribute. Code an instance of the class and
call the method.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SY" class="heading_s3BT">

14.4.4 Hierarchical Inheritance

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

This type of Inheritance is achieved when we have only one base class
and we created multiple derived classes using that single base. The
feature of base class is inherited by multiple derived classes.

</div>

<div class="class_s3BW">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s382">

class Base\_Class:

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

body of base class

</div>

<div class="class_s39D">

class Derived\_Class\_1(Base\_Class):

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

body of derived class

</div>

<div class="class_s39D">

class Dervied\_Class\_2(Base\_Class):

</div>

<div class="class_s12X">

body of derived class

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_196" class="class_sEY">

In the following diagram, Classes are represented as boxes. The
inheritance relationship is represented by an arrow from the base class
pointing to two different derived classes.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

![](Image00488.jpg){.class_s3C8} Recalling the above example, Now we
have a base class named <span class="class_s4UC">Father().</span> Inside
it we assign a keyword <span class="class_s4UC">None</span> to it. Also
we have a method <span class="class_s4UC">def father</span> inside the
body of a class as following, ![](Image00489.jpg){.class_s3CC}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we have a derived class named <span
class="class_s4UC">Son\_1().</span> In this class, we have a method
<span class="class_s4UC">parent().</span> Inside the function <span
class="class_s4UC">parent()</span> we also write print statement ­which
returning value of <span class="class_s4UC">self.fathername.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sNV-1">

![](Image00490.jpg){.class_sNV-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We have another derived class <span class="class_s4UC">Son\_2</span> of
the base class as follows,

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_197" class="class_s3CN-1">

![](Image00491.jpg){.class_s3CN-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we define two instances, <span class="class_s4UC">s1</span> for the
derived class <span class="class_s4UC">Son\_1</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">s2</span> for derived class <span
class="class_s4UC">Son\_2</span> . We also assigned string value <span
class="class_s4UC">Ben</span> to the variable <span
class="class_s4UC">fathername.</span>

</div>

![](Image00492.jpg){.class_s1EJ-1}

<div class="class_s7V">
