class="class_s4UC">s1</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">s2.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We get the following output by calling the method <span
class="class_s4UC">parent()</span> from the derived class <span
class="class_s4UC">Son\_1</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Son\_2.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sKN-1">

![](Image00493.jpg){.class_sKN-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let’s do another example. We have a super class named as <span
class="class_s4UC">Pologon ().</span> As polygon has common features
width and height so, we define the both variable and initialize them
with keyword <span class="class_s4UC">None</span> in class.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In the super class we also define a function <span
class="class_s4UE">set\_values</span> and use the method to set the
values of both variables. Also this method will take two arguments i-e
length and width.

</div>

<div class="class_s1R6">

def set\_values (self ,length ,width)

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_198" class="class_s7V">

We cannot inherit the private members of super class to sub class. As
both the variables <span class="class_s4UC">\_\_length</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">\_\_width</span> are private members of class <span
class="class_s4UC">Polygon</span> . This is called encapsulation. We
will study it in detail in the next section

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00494.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

So to access private members we use <span
class="class_s4UC">get()</span> method. We can write it as the following
code,

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

<span class="class_s4UC">Triangle</span> . So they can inherit some
properties from super class <span class="class_s4UC">Polygon.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now, we define a sub class <span class="class_s4UC">Rectangle</span>

<span class="class_s4UC">Polygon</span> class. So it can also use the
members of the <span class="class_s4UE">Polygon.</span>

<div id="text00014.html#a4SZ" class="heading_s81">

14.4.5 Hybrid Inheritance

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Hybrid Inheritance consists of multiple types of inheritances.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00502.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s3BW">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s3EC">

class Base\_Class:

</div>

<div class="class_s3EE">

body of base class

</div>

<div class="class_s3EC">

class Derived\_Class\_1(Base\_Class):

</div>

<div class="class_s3EH">

body of derived class

</div>

<div class="class_s3EC">

class Dervied\_Class\_2(Base\_Class):

</div>

<div class="class_s3EH">

body of derived class

</div>

<div class="class_s3EN">

class Derived\_Class\_3(Derived\_Class\_1,Derived\_Class\_2)

</div>

<div class="class_s3ER">

body of derived class

</div>

<div class="class_s3ET">

In the following diagram, Classes are represented as boxes. The <span
id="text00014.html#page_202"></span> inheritance relationship is
represented by an arrow from the base class pointing to the two
different derived classes. And another, derived class is inherited from
these two derived classes.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_203" class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00503.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

class="class_s4UC">Base</span> <span class="class_s4UE">.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_204" class="class_sWS-1">

![](Image00504.jpg){.class_sWS-0}

class="class_s4UC">Intermediate\_1,</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00505.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

inherited from class Base,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00506.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

<div id="text00014.html#a4T0" class="heading_sBN">

14.5 Encapsulation

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

As the word says, it encloses something in it like a capsule. When we
make any sub class then it can easily access every variable or method of
super class. So if we want to keep it private?

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

For keeping them private we use the concept of encapsulation.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00510.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_206" class="class_s7V">

We will see how to make

</div>

-   Private variable
-   Private method

<div class="class_s7V">

To make a variable private we use two underscore before the variable
name. In the following, we have a class name <span
class="class_s4UC">Car</span> . Here the attribute <span
class="class_s4UC">self.\_\_engine</span> is the private attribute
because we use underscore with it.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00511.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we define instance <span class="class_s4UC">Car\_1</span> of class
<span class="class_s4UC">Car().</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sH7-1">

![](Image00512.jpg){.class_sH7-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we call the method <span class="class_s4UC">get\_description</span>
from the class <span class="class_s4UC">Car.</span> This method
returning the attribute <span class="class_s4UC">self.make</span> and
<span class="class_s4UC">self.car</span> from the class and prints the
statement as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00513.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We know that engine is the private attribute of the class <span
class="class_s4UC">Car</span> . It means that we can’t access it. If we
try we get an error like the following

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_207" class="class_sWS-1">

![](Image00514.jpg){.class_sWS-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we see that how we can make a method private. For that we again use
two underscores <span class="class_s4UE">(\_\_)</span> before the method
name.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Again looking above example,

</div>

<div class="class_sH7-1">

![](Image00515.jpg){.class_sH7-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we define a method <span class="class_s4UC">def\_\_engine</span>
(self) which is private because of using underscores with it.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we define instance <span class="class_s4UC">Car\_1</span> of class
<span class="class_s4UC">Car()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sGW-0">

![](Image00516.jpg){.class_sGW-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Again calling the method <span
class="class_s4UC">get\_description</span> from the class <span
class="class_s4UC">Car</span> . This method returning the attribute
<span class="class_s4UC">self.make</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">self.car</span> from the <span
id="text00014.html#page_208"></span> class and prints the statement as
follows

</div>

<div class="class_s3CN-1">

![](Image00517.jpg){.class_s3CN-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now if we call method <span class="class_s4UC">\_\_engine</span> from
the class <span class="class_s4UC">Car().</span> Then we can’t able to
access and following error will generates,

</div>

<div class="class_s3H2-0">

![](Image00518.jpg){.class_s3H2-1}

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4T2" class="heading_s1RA">

14.6 Polymorphism

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_210" class="class_s79">

Polymorphism is a very important concept in programming. It is a Greek
word. As <span class="class_s4UE">Poly</span> means many and <span
class="class_s4UE">morphism</span> means forms so polymorphism means
many forms. In python it means that we use same function name but the
functions uses different signatures for different types.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">Information</span> : Its also allows us to use
similar names of method in derived class as used in base class

</div>

<div class="class_sEY">

The following methods are used for polymorphism:

</div>

-   Polymorphism with functions and objects
-   Polymorphism with Class Methods
-   Polymorphism with Inheritance

<div class="class_s7V">

We will see all these methods one by one.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4T3" class="heading_s81">

14.6.1 Polymorphism with functions and objects

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In this method of polymorphism, we can create a function that is able to
take any kind of object.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let’s do an example related to Polymorphism using functions and objects.
Here we a class <span class="class_s4UC">Car().</span> In <span
class="class_s4UC">Car()</span> we have three method defined <span
class="class_s4UC">company() , model()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">color()</span> as follows

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00523.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Also we have another class <span class="class_s4UC">Bike().</span> <span
id="text00014.html#page_211"></span> This class also have three methods
having the same name as class <span class="class_s4UC">Car()</span> i-e
<span class="class_s4UC">company(), model()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">color()</span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00524.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we created a function called <span class="class_s4UC">func()</span>
which will take an object named as obj. Now we call the methods <span
class="class_s4UC">company(), model()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">color()</span> each of which is defined in the above
two classes i-e <span class="class_s4UC">Car()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Bike()</span> ![](Image00525.jpg){.class_s3JF}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In the following block, we created instances <span
class="class_s4UC">car</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">bike</span>
of the classes <span class="class_s4UC">Car()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Bike()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s1FE-1">

![](Image00526.jpg){.class_s1FE-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we call both instances i-e <span class="class_s4UC">car</span> and
<span class="class_s4UC">bike</span> which gives us the following
output,

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_212" class="class_sZJ-0">

![](Image00527.jpg){.class_sZJ-1}

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4T4" class="heading_s81">

14.6.2 Polymorphism with Class Methods

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In this method we will see that how python can use our different defined
class types in similar way. In this method, first we create <span
class="class_s4UE">for loop</span> that iterates though a tuple of
objects. After that, we will call that method. As we assume that all
these methods actually exists in each of the defined class.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let’s do an example,

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we have class <span class="class_s4UC">Female()</span> having
attributes <span class="class_s4UC">name</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">age.</span> Also we have three methods in it named as
<span class="class_s4UC">info, welcome</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">goodbye</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_213" class="class_s3JZ-1">

![](Image00528.jpg){.class_s3JZ-0}

</div>

<div class="class_sEY">

We defined another class <span class="class_s4UC">Male()</span> having
attributes <span class="class_s4UC">name</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">age</span> . Also the methods use in this class
having same names as in class <span class="class_s4UE">Female()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s23F-1">

![](Image00529.jpg){.class_s23F-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

First we created instances <span class="class_s4UC">f1</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">m1</span> of classes <span
class="class_s4UC">Female()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Male().</span> Now we call the above two classes by
passing values of attributes. Here string values <span
class="class_s4UC">Maria</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">22</span>
assigned to attribute <span class="class_s4UC">name</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">age</span> of class <span
class="class_s4UC">Female().</span> Similarly, <span
class="class_s4UC">Adrian</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">18</span>
assigned to attributes <span class="class_s4UC">name</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">age</span> of class <span
id="text00014.html#page_214"></span> <span
class="class_s4UC">Male()</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00530.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we created <span class="class_s4UE">for loop</span> which will
iterates through the tuple of instances i-e <span
class="class_s4UC">f1</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">m1</span> .
When for loop iterates it calls the methods of these classes i-e <span
class="class_s4UC">info, welcome</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">goodbye</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

This loop executed for both classes <span
class="class_s4UC">Female()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">Male().</span> When we run the program, we get the
following output

</div>

<div class="class_sGW-0">

![](Image00531.jpg){.class_sGW-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

It refers to the use of a single type entity (method, operator or
object) to represent different types in different scenarios.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4T5" class="heading_s81">

14.6.3 Polymorphism with Inheritance

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In this method, we use methods name for derived class same as used for
base class. Till now we learnt that the derived class inherited all the
methods and attributes from the parent class. But here we see that we
can also modify those methods.

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#a4VK" class="heading_s7B">

14.6.3.1 Method Overriding

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

It means that if we want to redefine certain attribute or method in the
child class specifically to fit the child class.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let do an example of this method of inheritance. Here we have a derived
class <span class="class_s4UC">Bird().</span> In this class we have
methods <span class="class_s4UC">intro()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">flight()</span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00532.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we have derived class <span class="class_s4UC">Crow</span> having
only one method as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sH7-1">

![](Image00533.jpg){.class_sH7-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Following we have another derived class <span
class="class_s4UC">Emu</span> also having only one method.

</div>

<div class="class_sGW-0">

![](Image00534.jpg){.class_sGW-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we have defined instances of base class and derived classes.
Instance <span class="class_s4UC">obj\_bird</span> for class <span
class="class_s4UC">Bird(),</span> <span
class="class_s4UC">obj\_cro</span> for class <span
class="class_s4UC">Crow()</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">obj\_emu</span> for class <span
class="class_s4UC">Emu().</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_216" class="class_s7V">

We can write the following code,

</div>

<div class="class_sNV-1">

![](Image00535.jpg){.class_sNV-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In this block of code we call different methods which will give us the
following outputs,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00536.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

-   As <span class="class_s4UC">obj\_bird</span> is the instance of
    <span class="class_s4UC">Bird()</span> so in first two lines when we
    call method <span class="class_s4UC">intro</span> and <span
    class="class_s4UC">flight</span> of base class <span
    class="class_s4UC">Bird</span> then, it prints the
    respective statements.
-   Note when we call the method <span class="class_s4UC">intro</span>
    of the derived classes <span class="class_s4UC">Crow()</span> (in
    line 3) and <span class="class_s4UC">Emu()</span> ( in line 5) ,they
    used the methods from base class <span
    class="class_s4UC">Bird()</span> and prints the statement as

<div class="class_s3MB">

There are many types of birds.

</div>

-   But when we call the method <span class="class_s4UC">flight()</span>
    of derived classes <span class="class_s4UC">Crow()</span> (in
    line 4) and <span class="class_s4UC">Emu()</span> ( in line 6) then
    they override the print message.
-   The both classes prints their own print statement defined in the
    method <span class="class_s4UC">flight()</span> <span
    id="text00014.html#page_217"></span> rather than printing the
    statement defined in the method of base class.

<div id="text00014.html#a4T6" class="heading_sBN">

14.7 Overloading Operators

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In python, we have a lot of overloading operators. Let do an example,

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we have a class named it as <span
class="class_s4UC">Vector()</span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s23F-1">

![](Image00537.jpg){.class_s23F-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Note that we use <span class="class_s4UC">\_\_add\_\_</span> method in
the class to add <span class="class_s4UC">vectors</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In the following block we pass the values representing the dimension of
vectors and get the following output,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00538.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Similarly, we have other overload operations in the following table<span
class="class_s4VD">,</span>

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_218" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00539.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_219" class="class_s3MZ">

Similarly, we have comparison and unary operators as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s3N3-1">

![](Image00540.jpg){.class_s3N3-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s3N7-1">

![](Image00541.jpg){.class_s3N7-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s3N9">

<span class="class_s4UF">In python</span> we also have some overload
method i-e

</div>

<div class="class_s3NB">

\_\_init\_\_ ( self \[,args...\] )

</div>

<div id="text00014.html#page_220" class="class_s3N9">

This is a constructor (with any optional arguments)\
<span class="class_s4UE">\_\_del\_\_( self )</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s3NE">

This is destructor able to deletes an object

</div>

<div class="class_s3NG">

\_\_repr\_\_( self )

</div>

<div class="class_s2VW">

This able to evaluates string representation

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

\_\_str\_\_( self )

</div>

<div class="class_s2VW">

This able to print string representation

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

\_\_cmp\_\_ ( self, x )

</div>

<div class="class_s14Y">

This is used for object comparison.

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4T7" class="heading_sDR">

Chapter 15 : Data Files

</div>

<div class="class_sDT">

Till now, we covered all major topics of Python. We created variable,
list, dictionaries, define the classes, work on loops etc.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

But all the values generated during programming or execution of programs
will disappeared after the program close. All these values, variables
not stored permanently.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00542.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Can we write all the values generated through code to the data file? So
when our program closes we just go to that data file to read the text.
In this chapter we see how to do this all.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We can read the data from the files and can also write data in the
files.

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4T8" class="heading_sBN">

15.1 Reading and Writing in external file from Python code

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In python the file operation takes place in these following steps

</div>

-   Open the file
-   Read or write in the file
-   Close the file

<div class="class_s7V">

We can read and write files by using a function <span
id="text00015.html#page_222"></span> <span class="class_s4UE">with
open().</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Syntax:  

</div>

<div class="class_s1R6">

with open(“file\_name.txt”, “mode”)as file:

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

This function needs the following two parameters,

</div>

-   <span class="class_s4UE">File name</span>

<div class="class_s3PH">

The name of file which we want to access.

</div>

-   <span class="class_s4UE">Mode</span>

<div class="class_s3PH">

In this parameter python decide that whether we have to read the data
from file <span class="class_s4UC">file\_name.txt</span> or have to
write the data to the file <span
class="class_s4UC">file\_name.txt</span> . There are three basic modes,

</div>

-   Read
-   Write
-   Append

<div class="class_s7V">

Note that the comma<span class="class_s4UE">(,)</span> followed by
parameter <span class="class_s4UE">mode</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The <span class="class_s4UE">as</span> in the syntax is a keyword
returns a handler to the file. Python needs a handle in order to get
into the file. In this case, I've given it a handle named <span
class="class_s4UE">file.</span> The line ends with the colon <span
class="class_s4UE">(:)</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00543.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4T9" class="heading_s8K">

15.1.1 Writing to text file

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

We have to write the writing mode as w

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s39D">

with open(“my\_file.txt”, “w”)as file:

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

file.write(“This is my file”)

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we pass the file named <span class="class_s4UE">my\_file.txt</span>
. The line 2 starts with the name of file handle we specified in line 1,
then a dot<span class="class_s4UE">(.)</span> followed by keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">write().</span> Inside the parenthesis we write
string which we want to store in the file.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00544.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00545.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

First this writing mode will create a file and named it as <span
class="class_s4UC">new\_file.txt</span> and write <span
class="class_s4UC">Hello! Data Files.</span> in the file.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Also we can use this mode by storing a string in a variable. First we
store string in the variable <span class="class_s4UC">intro</span> as
follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sH7-1">

![](Image00546.jpg){.class_sH7-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Then we pass the variable <span class="class_s4UC">intro</span> in the
method <span class="class_s4UC">write,</span> <span
id="text00015.html#page_224"></span> as following,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00547.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4TA" class="heading_s81">

15.1.2 Reading from the text file

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The reading mode is represented by <span class="class_s4UE">r</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax:</span> We pass two parameters in the
function <span class="class_s4UE">with open().</span> The line 2 starts
with the name of a variable, then name of file handle <span
class="class_s4UC">file</span> , then a dot<span
class="class_s4UE">(.)</span> followed by keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">read().</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

with open(“file\_name.txt”, “r”)as file:

</div>

<div class="class_s3RU">

content =file.read()

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The function <span class="class_s4UC">read()</span> will read all the
data from the file named <span class="class_s4UC">my\_file.txt</span>
and saved to the variable <span class="class_s4UC">content,</span>  
then we print the variable <span class="class_s4UC">content</span> which
shows all the data of the file.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00548.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_sH7-1">

![](Image00549.jpg){.class_sH7-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we read the data from the file <span
class="class_s4UC">new\_file.txt</span> created above. This shows the
text inside that file.

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4TB" class="heading_s81">

15.1.3 Writing in the append mode

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Append mode is represented by “a”.

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s3S7">

with open(“file\_name.txt, “a”)as file:

</div>

<div class="class_s382">

file.write(“This text is written is append mode”)

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

When we use the mode write <span class="class_s4UE">“w”</span> the
function <span class="class_s4UE">with open</span> opens the file and
write the text. When we get out of the body of function <span
class="class_s4UC">with open(),</span> then the file will automatically
close. Now if we have to write more text to same file then the previous
text will disappeared and replaced by new text.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

If we want previous as well new text in that file, then we will use
append mode. As append mode allows us to write further.

</div>

<div class="class_sWS-1">

![](Image00550.jpg){.class_sWS-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we don’t want to remove the previous text and want to write more
text to same file <span class="class_s4UC">new\_file.txt.</span> Now we
see that the new text don’t over write the previous text “Hello! Data
Files<span class="class_s4UC">.”</span> but we further add the text “Now
I am writing this text in append mode”.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00551.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We see that the text added to the <span class="class_s4UC">file
new\_file.txt</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We have further modes:

</div>

-   <div id="text00015.html#page_226">

    </div>

    w+
-   r+
-   a+

<div id="text00015.html#a4TC" class="heading_s81">

15.1.4 w+ mode

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The w+ mode also allows us both to read the file as well as write the
data in the file.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

If the file not exists then w+ mode first create a file of that name
then write the data to it.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we just created a new file named it as <span
class="class_s4UC">new\_file\_1.</span> First the file will create and
the text “In this mode we can read and read the text” added to that
file, works same as <span class="class_s4UE">w</span> mode.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00552.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Note that, we print the function <span
class="class_s4UC">file.read()</span> but nothing print. The reason is
that the call <span class="class_s4UC">file.read()</span> will try to
read from the end of the file and returns the empty string.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

So we use the method <span class="class_s4UE">seek().</span> This method
sets the current position of the pointer at the offset. As we pass zero
so it sets to index zero. We can write as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00553.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Great! We printed the text in the file

</div>

<div class="heading_s81">

<div id="text00015.html#toc147_">

![](Image00554.jpg){.class_sRG}

</div>

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4TE" class="heading_s30F">

15.1.5 r+ mode

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The r+ mode allows us both to read the file and write in the file.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In mode works for the existing files.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00555.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_sXW-1">

![](Image00556.jpg){.class_sXW-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we also use the method <span class="class_s4UE">seek()</span> to
set the current position of the pointer at zero index.

</div>

<div class="class_sEY">

![](Image00557.jpg){#page_229 .class_s3TS} <span
class="class_s4UC">              In this mode we can read and write the
text.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4TF" class="heading_s81">

15.1.6 a+ mode

</div>

<div class="class_s3TV">

This mode opens a file for both appending and reading. The file pointer
is at the end of the file if the file exists. The file opens in the
append mode.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00558.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4V8">In this mode, text is not over write but
further added to the file like appending mode</span> <span
class="class_s4V9">a</span>

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#page_230" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00559.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s3U4">

We have other modes in the following table

</div>

  -------------------------- -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  <div class="class_s3U6">   <div class="class_s3U9">
                             
  Modes                      Description
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s3UE">   <div class="class_s3UH">
                             
  x                          Opens a file for exclusive creation. If the file already exists then this mode create an error.
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s3UE">   <div class="class_s3UH">
                             
  t                          Opens a file in text mode
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s3UE">   <div class="class_s3UH">
                             
  b                          Opens the file in binary mode
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s3UE">   <div class="class_s3V1">
                             
  rb                         Use for reading a binary file.
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s3UE">   <div class="class_s3V1">
                             
  rb+                        For reading or writing a binary file
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s3UE">   <div class="class_s3V1">
                             
  wb                         Opens a file for writing only in binary format. Overwrites the file if the file exists.
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s3UE">   <div class="class_s3V1">
                             
  wb+                        For writing a binary file
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s3UE">   <div class="class_s3V1">
                             
  ab+                        Opens a file for both appending and reading in binary format.
                             
  </div>                     </div>
  -------------------------- -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

<div class="class_s3VV">

Task: Write a programme using all modes given in the above table one by
one.        

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4TG" class="heading_s3VX">

Chapter 16 : Modules

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In this chapter we will discuss that what actually modules are? Why we
need it? Imagine that we have a file having a lot of variables, classes
and function. This all will create a mess and we as a programmer get
confused, so we stored these functions in a separate file called <span
class="class_s4UE">Module.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Module is same as code library. It helps us to logically organise our
Python code. With the help of module,

</div>

-   We group related code to module which make easier to understand
    and use.
-   We write a function once and call it from other programs.
-   We can use code written by other coders by writing their modules.

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax:</span> We can give any name to the file
we like. When we save the file we use extension <span
class="class_s4UE">.py</span> with the name of the file.

</div>

<div class="class_s3W7">

my\_file.py

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4TH" class="heading_sBN">

16.1 Functions in module

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In this section, we will discuss that how to create a module consist of
functions and how we can use that module.

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4TJ" class="heading_s81">

16.1.1 Creating a module

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

To create a module we just use extension <span
class="class_s4UC">.py</span> . Let’s do an example.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In the following block of code we defined a function <span
class="class_s4UC">greeting</span>

</div>

<div class="class_sGW-0">

![](Image00560.jpg){.class_sGW-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We saved this text file and named it as <span
id="text00015.html#page_232"></span> <span
class="class_s4UC">greet.py</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let’s create another module.

</div>

<div class="class_s3WN-0">

![](Image00561.jpg){.class_s3WN-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we defined four basic math operations. We save this text file named
it <span class="class_s4UC">operations.py</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00562.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#a4TK" class="heading_s81">

16.1.2 Use a module

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Now we can use the module we created above by using keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">import</span> .

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

First we open another code file then load the module by using the
following syntax,

</div>

<div class="class_s1R6">

load.file\_name.py

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

First we write load then a dot <span class="class_s4UE">(.)</span>
followed by file name. Here we load the module named <span
class="class_s4UC">greet.py</span> as follows,

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#page_233" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00563.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

By running the above line, all the code loaded in the block as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00564.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00565.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we import the module which we loaded, by using the keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">import</span>  

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00566.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We called the greeting function by passing the string <span
class="class_s4UC">Ainne</span>

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#page_234" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00567.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In the following, we load the module named <span
class="class_s4UC">operations.py</span> which we created above,
![](Image00568.jpg){.class_s3XN}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In the following block we import this module,

</div>

<div class="class_sXW-1">

![](Image00569.jpg){.class_sXW-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00570.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00015.html#page_235" class="class_s7V">

Now we can call any function in the module. In this module we have four
functions i-e <span class="class_s4UC">add(), sub(), mul()</span> and
<span class="class_s4UC">div().</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

In the following block we call the function <span
class="class_s4UC">add</span> by passing the integer values <span
class="class_s4UC">2</span> and <span class="class_s4UC">3,</span> which
gives us output by adding both values.

</div>

<div class="class_sKN-1">

![](Image00571.jpg){.class_sKN-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we call function <span class="class_s4UC">div()</span> by passing
integer values <span class="class_s4UC">4</span> and <span
class="class_s4UC">5</span> .This function will give us the output by
dividing them i-e as <span class="class_s4UC">4</span> dividing by <span
class="class_s4UC">5</span> equals to <span
class="class_s4UC">0.8</span>

</div>

![](Image00572.jpg){.class_s23F-0}

![](Image00573.jpg){.class_s3Y9-1}

Chapter 17 : CSV Files

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Like in the previous chapter, where we write the data through python
code in the text file, we can also write data in CSV files.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

CSV stands for <span class="class_s4UE">comma separated values.</span>
It means that separator of each value is comma. We write comma after
writing the first value then write the second value put a comma then
write third value and so on.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00591.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

CSV files are basically simplified version of the spreadsheet or
database.

</div>

<div class="class_s41U">

Here is the excel file, 

</div>

  -------------------------- -------------------------- -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  <div class="class_s41W">   <div class="class_s420">   <div class="class_s424">
                                                        
  Year                       Club                       Winner
                                                        
  </div>                     </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s429">   <div class="class_s42C">   <div class="class_s42F">
                                                        
  2015                       Barcelona                  [Lionel Messi](https://www.topendsports.com/sport/soccer/profiles/messi-lionel.htm)
                                                        
  </div>                     </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s429">   <div class="class_s42C">   <div class="class_s42F">
                                                        
  2016                       Real Madrid                Cristiano Ronaldo
                                                        
  </div>                     </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s429">   <div class="class_s42C">   <div class="class_s42F">
                                                        
  2017                       Real Madrid                Cristiano Ronaldo
                                                        
  </div>                     </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s429">   <div class="class_s42C">   <div class="class_s42F">
                                                        
  2018                       Real Madrid                LokaModric
                                                        
  </div>                     </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s429">   <div class="class_s42C">   <div class="class_s42F">
                                                        
  2019                       Barcelona                  [Lionel Messi](https://www.topendsports.com/sport/soccer/profiles/messi-lionel.htm)
                                                        
  </div>                     </div>                     </div>
  -------------------------- -------------------------- -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

<div class="class_sDT">

Now we can import above excel file as a CSV file. So the CSV file looks
like as follows,

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_243" class="class_s43J">

Year, Club, Winner

</div>

<div class="class_s43M">

2015, Barcelona, [Lionel
Messi](https://www.topendsports.com/sport/soccer/profiles/messi-lionel.htm)

</div>

<div class="class_s43M">

2016, Real Madrid, Cristiano Ronaldo

</div>

<div class="class_s43M">

2017, Real Madrid, Cristiano Ronaldo

</div>

<div class="class_s43M">

2018, Real Madrid, Loka Modric

</div>

<div class="class_s43M">

2019, Barcelona, [Lionel
Messi](https://www.topendsports.com/sport/soccer/profiles/messi-lionel.htm)

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00592.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We can do the following three things in CSV files as we did in text
files

</div>

-   Read
-   Write
-   Append

<div id="text00016.html#a4TW" class="heading_sBN">

17.1 Reading the CSV files

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If a CSV file exists we can read the data from it easily.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax:</span> First we import <span
class="class_s4UE">csv,</span> then open the file using function <span
class="class_s4UE">with open().</span> Also, we have to assign a file
handle i-e <span class="class_s4UE">file</span> . With the help of this
file handle, python will access the data of the CSV file. In line 3 we
define a variable which equals to the function <span
id="text00016.html#page_244"></span> <span
class="class_s4UC">csv.reader.</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s445">

<span class="class_s4V5">import csv</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s1R6">

with open(file\_name.csv)as file:

</div>

<div class="class_s1R6">

variable = csv.reader(file)

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Note that we pass the file handle <span class="class_s4UC">file</span>
as an argument.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00593.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We use the following syntax to make the data useable.

</div>

<div class="class_s3A9">

<span class="class_s4V5">with open(“my\_file”) as file:</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s44F">

content = csv.reader(file)

</div>

<div class="class_s44F">

content\_of\_competetion=\[\]

</div>

<div class="class_s39B">

foreach\_line in content:

</div>

<div class="class_s44K">

content\_of\_competetion+=each\_line

</div>

<div class="class_s44K">

print(content\_of\_competetion)

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We use <span class="class_s4UC">for</span> loop to extract all data
lines in the form of list.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Here we created empty list <span
class="class_s4UC">content\_of\_competition</span> <span
id="text00016.html#page_245"></span> . We are appending each line which
is coming from CSV file <span class="class_s4UC">content</span> in the
list <span class="class_s4UC">content\_of\_competition</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let’s do an example. We write the following data into text file and
named it as <span class="class_s4UE">competition.csv</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00594.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We first import <span class="class_s4UE">csv</span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s3ZH-0">

![](Image00595.jpg){.class_s3ZH-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now we open csv file <span class="class_s4UC">competition.csv</span> by
using a function <span class="class_s4UC">with open.</span> Python will
access the data of the CSV file with the help of file handle i-e <span
class="class_s4UC">file</span> . We define a variable <span
class="class_s4UC">content</span> which equals to the function <span
class="class_s4UC">csv.reader()</span> . Now with the help of <span
class="class_s4UC">for loop,</span> we extracted data and print it.

</div>

<div class="class_sZJ-0">

![](Image00596.jpg){.class_sZJ-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We run the above block of code which gives us the following output,

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_246" class="class_s36Z-0">

![](Image00597.jpg){.class_s36Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00598.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_sEY">

Note that the output data is in the form of multiple lists. So we merge
all of data into single list by defining the empty list i-e <span
class="class_s4UC">competition</span> as following,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00599.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

By running this, we will get the output as follows

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_247" class="class_sDB-0">

![](Image00600.jpg){.class_sDB-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Great!

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00601.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#a4TX" class="heading_s2CJ">

17.1.1 Picking information out of them

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Python is able to pick some specific value from the given list.
Recalling the above example in which we have a list <span
class="class_s4UC">competition.</span> Now if we pass any index the
python displays the value of that index. For example<span
class="class_s4UC">,</span> by passing the index <span
class="class_s4UC">3</span> in the list <span
class="class_s4UC">competition</span> gives the value <span
class="class_s4UC">2015</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00602.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Similarly, by passing the index <span class="class_s4UC">10</span> in
the competition give value <span class="class_s4UC">Real Madrid</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s23F-1">

![](Image00603.jpg){.class_s23F-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00604.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We can also get the index number of any value in the list competition as
follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00605.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_249" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00606.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let’s do something useful by using the concept of index.

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00607.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We give the input as the string value <span
class="class_s4UC">Barcelona</span> <span class="class_s4V5">.</span>

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_250" class="class_sH7-1">

![](Image00608.jpg){.class_sH7-0}

</div>

-   First, we defined the user input and stored it to the variable <span
    class="class_s4UC">club</span> .
-   Then the index value of string i-e <span
    class="class_s4UC">Barcelona</span> stored in the variable <span
    class="class_s4UC">index\_number\_of\_club.</span>
-   We know that the name of player is stored next to the club name so
    we add <span class="class_s4UC">1</span> to the index of club name
    i-e <span class="class_s4UC">Index\_number\_of\_club.</span>
-   Now the python looks the value against the <span
    class="class_s4UC">index\_number\_of\_winner</span> in the list
    competition and stored the name in the variable <span
    class="class_s4UC">winner.</span>

<div class="class_s7V">

At last, we print this line of code, which gives us the following
output,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00609.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

class="class_s4UC">winner</span> by entering the <span

increment value. i-e <span class="class_s4UC">2</span> .We can write the

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_251" class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00610.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

<div id="text00016.html#a4TY" class="heading_sBN">

17.2 Writing in the CSV files

</div>

<div class="class_s47W">

We can load data to any csv file by defining the name of that csv file.

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_252" class="class_sJP-1">

![](Image00612.jpg){.class_sJP-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The syntax is almost same as for reading a CSV file. Just we pass
parameter <span class="class_s4UC">w</span> (in quotation marks) for
writing data in it. Also we have to define a file handle. We call the
function <span class="class_s4UE">writer</span> in the csv module.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The parameter <span class="class_s4UE">newline</span> (used in the
syntax) having the value <span class="class_s4UE">None</span> by
default. It generates empty line between two rows. We can remove that
line.

</div>

<div class="class_s484">

newline = “”

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

For technical reasons, we can't write data directly to the CSV file. So
we defined a variable, and give any legal name to it. Then, the variable
connected by a dot to the keyword <span
class="class_s4UE">writerow</span> . Each row is loaded into the handler
as a list.

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_253" class="class_s487">

import csv

</div>

<div class="class_s487">

with open(“my\_file”, “w”, newline= “”) as file:

</div>

<div class="class_s48A">

variable\_name=csv.writer(file, delimiter= “,”)

</div>

<div class="class_s48A">

variable\_name.writerow(\[“Year”, “champion”, “top score”\]

</div>

<div class="class_s48A">

variable\_name.writerow(\[“Year 1”, “champion 1”, “top score 1”\])

</div>

<div class="class_s48A">

variable\_name.writerow(\[“Year 2”, “champion 2”, “top score 2”\])

</div>

<div class="class_s48A">

variable\_name.writerow(\[“Year 3”, “champion 3”, “top score 3”\])

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00613.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Let’s do an example. We want to create a list of FIFA World Cup Records.

</div>

-   First the file <span class="class_s4UC">com.csv</span> is created as
    the file of this name doesnot exists 
-   We name the variable <span class="class_s4UC">data\_handler</span>
-   Then we writes five rows using the function <span
    id="text00016.html#page_254"></span> <span
    class="class_s4UC">writerow()</span>

<div class="class_sU4">

![](Image00614.jpg){.class_s48V} <span class="class_s4VS">­­</span>

</div>

17.3 Appending to CSV files

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We can append more data to existing file without removing the previous
data.

</div>

<div class="class_s49H-0">

![](Image00619.jpg){.class_s49H-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax</span> : We can use <span
class="class_s4UC">a,</span> for appending data into file.

</div>

<div class="class_s49M">

import csv

</div>

<div class="class_s49M">

with open(“my\_file”, “a”, newline= “”) as file:

</div>

<div class="class_s48A">

variable\_name=csv.writer(file, delimiter= “,”)

</div>

<div class="class_s48A">

variable\_name.writerow(\[“Year 4”, “champion 4”, “top score 4”\])

</div>

<div class="class_s48A">

variable\_name.writerow(\[“Year 5”, “champion 5”, “top score 5”\])

</div>

<div class="class_sEY">

Let’s do an example. Recalling the previous example in which we created
the file <span class="class_s4UC">competitions.csv</span> . Now we can
append more data to that file by the following way,

</div>

<div id="text00016.html#page_256" class="class_sH7-1">

![](Image00620.jpg){.class_sH7-0}

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00621.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Great! The new rows appended in the same file.

</div>

<div id="text00017.html#a4TZ" class="heading_sDR">

Chapter 18 : JSON files

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

In chapter 17, we deal CSV files. In this chapter, we will see another
file format Json.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Json stands for <span class="class_s4UE">JavaScript Object
Notation</span> . As name says that it is something related to
JavaScript but python programmers can also use this.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Recalling some concept from chapter 15, where we discussed about writing
the data in the text file as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00622.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

We can read the data from the file <span
class="class_s4UC">text.txt</span> as following,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00623.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now, we want to add a list rather than a string so, we first define a
list <span class="class_s4UC">number</span> and then we write in the
text file using function <span class="class_s4UC">with open()</span> as
follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00624.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00017.html#page_258" class="class_s4AR">

But it will create the following error.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">TypeError: write() argument must be str, not
list</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s12J">

We can't save a Python list in a text file. You can only save a text
string in it. To save a list in a text file, we can use CSV file, but
best way is to use JSON file.

</div>

<div id="text00017.html#a4U0" class="heading_sBN">

18.1 Working with JSON

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

JSON file has functions same as CSV files. We can do the following in
JSON file,

</div>

-   Read the file
-   Write in the file
-   Append in the file

<div class="class_sU4">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax:</span> First we have to import module
json. Then with the help of function <span class="class_s4UC">with
open</span> we open a file.

</div>

<div class="class_sU4">

At last, we write a module name <span class="class_s4UE">json.</span>
Then, comes a dot followed by the function <span
class="class_s4UC">dump</span> . This function will takes two arguments
i-e the list name and the file handle

</div>

<div class="class_s4B3">

<span class="class_s4V5">import json</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s4B5">

list\_name = \["m1", "m2", "m3"\]

</div>

<div class="class_s4B5">

with open("my\_file.json", "w") as file:

</div>

<div class="class_s4B8">

json.dump(list\_name, file)

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<div id="text00017.html#page_259">

![](Image00625.jpg){.class_sRG}

</div>

</div>

<div class="class_s4BF">

                           <span
class="class_s4V5">print(json.dumps(object))</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s4BF">

We can convert the following types of Python objects

</div>

-   <span class="class_s4UR">dict</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UR">list</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UR">tuple</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UR">string</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UR">int</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UR">float</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UR">True</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UR">False</span>
-   <span class="class_s4UR">None</span>

<div class="class_s4C0">

When we convert python objects, we get the following json equivalent,

</div>

  -------------------------- -------------------------------------------------------
  <div class="class_s4C2">   <div class="class_s4C6">
                             
  Python                     Json
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div class="class_s4CD">
                             
  dict                       Object
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div class="class_s4CD">
                             
  list                       Array
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div class="class_s4CD">
                             
  tuple                      Array
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div class="class_s4CD">
                             
  string                     String
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div class="class_s4CD">
                             
  int                        Number
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div class="class_s4CD">
                             
  float                      Number
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div id="text00017.html#page_260" class="class_s4CD">
                             
  True                       true
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div class="class_s4CD">
                             
  False                      false
                             
  </div>                     </div>

  <div class="class_s4CA">   <div class="class_s4CD">
                             
  None                       null
                             
  </div>                     </div>
  -------------------------- -------------------------------------------------------

<div class="class_s4DW">

For example, the following give us the output null.

</div>

<div class="class_s4DY">

print(json.dumps(None))

</div>

<div id="text00017.html#a4U1" class="heading_s81">

18.1.3 Accessing the information from JSON files

<div class="class_s79">

class="class_s4UE">dictionary</span> from a <span

into JSON file we can read it easily.

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax:</span> We again use the function <span
class="class_s4UC">with open</span> and pass the file name as an
argument. Then we call the function <span
class="class_s4UC">load()</span> of the json module.

with open("my\_file.json") as f:

</div>

<div class="class_s4FH">

my\_file = json.load(f)

<div id="text00018.html#a4U3" class="heading_sDR">

Chapter 19 : Exception

</div>

<div class="class_sDT">

<span class="class_s4UE">Syntax errors</span> occur when compiler or
interpreter caught errors during compile or interpret

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">Exceptions</span> are run time errors. It means
that nothing wrong in program but from the user side.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

For example, developer writes a code which needs user defined input.
Assume that the code is perfectly correct but, the user gives wrong
input, which crash the whole code.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

As a developer, we must keep in mind that if this scenario happens, what
we must do something to protect the whole code.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Python manage the errors that arises during program execution by using
special objects known as <span class="class_s4UE">Exceptions</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00636.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#a4U4" class="heading_sBN">

19.1 Handling errors

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Errors/ Exception can be handle two keywords <span
class="class_s4UE">try</span> and <span class="class_s4UE">except</span>

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#a4U5" class="heading_s81">

19.1.1 Try block

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Programmers write main code in the try block.

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#a4U6" class="heading_s81">

19.1.2 Except block

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

Python executes the except block if things went wrong.

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s4H0">

try:

</div>

<div class="class_s4H2">

\#body of try block

</div>

<div class="class_s4H0">

except:

</div>

<div class="class_s4H5">

\#body of except block

</div>

<div class="class_s4H9-0">

![](Image00637.jpg){.class_s4H9-1}

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#page_267" class="class_sEY">

Let’s suppose we have a following code, in which the python program asks
about the file name from the user which will assign to variable <span
class="class_s4UC">filename.</span> The <span class="class_s4UC">with
open</span> function will open the file and function <span
class="class_s4UC">read</span> will read the content and display it

</div>

<div class="class_s4HE-1">

![](Image00638.jpg){.class_s4HE-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

To read the file, user must enter the file name.

</div>

<div class="class_sNV-1">

![](Image00639.jpg){.class_sNV-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The file <span class="class_s4UC">myfile</span> does not exists so it
make the following error,

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

FileNotFoundError: \[Errno 2\] No such file or directory: 'myfile.txt'

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

If you code an exception, then this gives the user a clearer error
message and also keeps the program from shutting down.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

So, we can write it as the following block,

</div>

<div class="class_sN2-1">

![](Image00640.jpg){.class_sN2-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

As the <span class="class_s4UC">try</span> <span
id="text00018.html#page_268"></span> block says that take file from user
then open it, after opening the file read the content in the file and
also display it

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The <span class="class_s4UC">except</span> block begins with the keyword
except, followed by the keyword <span
class="class_s4UC">FileNotFoundError</span> and a <span
class="class_s4UC">colon</span> . When the except block run, the print
statement inside its body will executed.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now if we enter again the non-existing file i-e <span
class="class_s4UC">myfile</span> then python display the following
message,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00641.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Now, in the following example the python again need input from the user.
First this code will display <span class="class_s4UE">Enter
numerator</span> . After taking the value of numerator it asks for the
denominator

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Note that we converted both input values to integer by using <span
class="class_s4UC">int,</span> as the type of input value is always
string.

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

The exception block will print the reason of an error.

</div>

<div class="class_sGW-0">

![](Image00642.jpg){.class_sGW-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Suppose if user enters the value <span class="class_s4UC">4</span> for
the numerator and <span class="class_s4UC">2</span> for denominator than
output will be,

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#page_269" class="class_sGW-0">

![](Image00643.jpg){.class_sGW-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Similarly, if user enters values <span class="class_s4UC">2</span> and
<span class="class_s4UC">10</span> then the output will be as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_sDB-0">

![](Image00644.jpg){.class_sDB-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Great!

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

But, what happened when user enters the value <span
class="class_s4UE">zero</span> for denominator?

</div>

<div class="class_sNV-1">

![](Image00645.jpg){.class_sNV-0}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

It gives a clear message that error occurs due to the value zero for
denominator and kept the whole program from dying.

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#a4U7" class="heading_s81">

19.1.3 Else Block

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The function of keyword <span class="class_s4UC">else</span> is to
define a block. This block will be executed if no error occurs.

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Syntax:

</div>

<div class="class_s4JS">

try:

</div>

<div class="class_s4H2">

\#body of try block

</div>

<div class="class_s4H0">

except <span id="text00018.html#page_270"></span> :

</div>

<div class="class_s4H5">

\#body of except block

</div>

<div class="class_s4H0">

else:

</div>

<div class="class_s4H5">

\#body of else block

</div>

<div class="class_s4K1-0">

![](Image00646.jpg){.class_s4K1-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Nothing wrong with the try block so else statement also executed. But if
the error errors it will not run the else block as follows

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00647.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#a4U8" class="heading_s81">

19.1.4 Finally Block

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

The keyword <span class="class_s4UC">finally</span> will also create a
block. This block will be executed regardless the error occur or not by
<span class="class_s4UC">try</span> block

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#page_271" class="class_s3BW">

Syntax:              

</div>

<div class="class_s4H0">

try:

</div>

<div class="class_s4H2">

\#body of try block

</div>

<div class="class_s4H0">

except :

</div>

<div class="class_s4H5">

\#body of except block

</div>

<div class="class_s4H0">

finally:

</div>

<div class="class_s4H5">

\#body of finally block

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

Like, here we are trying to open a file that is not writable,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00648.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div id="text00018.html#a4U9" class="heading_s1WF">

19.2 Loop through JSON

</div>

<div class="class_s79">

If the user put wrong input then the programme will show error message.
As, the programme should give another try to the user that he can enter
another input. Recalling the previous example, in which user enter wrong
value for the denominator. Now, he can enter another value for the
denominator. For that we can use the <span class="class_s4UE">while
loop</span> as follows,

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

<span class="class_s4UE">Hint:</span> The loop <span
class="class_s4UE">while True</span> will keep repeating the statement
until there is a <span class="class_s4UE">break</span> <span
id="text00018.html#page_272"></span> statement

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00649.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7V">

As long as the user enters wrong value there is no break statement. Now,
if user enters the value zero again for the denominator then the python
will ask again for new values as following,

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00650.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s7Z-0">

![](Image00651.jpg){.class_s7Z-1}

</div>

<div class="class_s18A">

Task:

</div>

<div class="class_s4M2">

<span class="class_s4US">1)</span> <span class="class_s4UU"> </span>
<span class="class_s4US">Write a code to open the file from your
desktop, read and display the content of the file with the help of
try-except block. Do this task using</span> <span
class="class_s4UV-0">while loop</span> <span class="class_s4US">to give
the user another chance</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s4M4">

<span class="class_s4US">(</span> <span
class="class_s4UV-0">Hint:</span> <span
id="text00018.html#page_273"></span> <span class="class_s4US">End while
loop with break statement)</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s4M6">

<span class="class_s4US">2)</span> <span class="class_s4UU"> </span>
<span class="class_s4US">Write the code beginning with the </span> <span
class="class_s4UV-0">while</span> <span class="class_s4US"> statement.
Try block will asks values of</span> <span class="class_s4UT">a</span>
<span class="class_s4US">and</span> <span class="class_s4UT">b</span>
<span class="class_s4US">from user. The</span> <span
class="class_s4UT">if statement</span> <span class="class_s4US">in try
block will tests whether </span> <span class="class_s4UT">a</span> <span
class="class_s4US"> divided by </span> <span class="class_s4UT">b</span>
<span class="class_s4US"> has a remainder of</span> <span
class="class_s4UT">0</span> <span class="class_s4US">. If so, display a
message “No reminder”. Also make up the message for exception</span>

</div>

<div class="class_s4M8">

<span class="class_s4US">(</span> <span
class="class_s4UV-0">Hint:</span> <span class="class_s4US">Focus on the
indentation level.)</span>

</div>

19.3 Raise

exception. For example, we as a programmer can raise an exception if
certain condition happened.
